01.996-.997h3c.348 0 .649.18.828.45l4.996 7.492c.11.148.168.347.168.55zm0 0"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></aside><main class="docMainContainer_TBSr"><div class="container padding-top--md padding-bottom--lg"><div class="row"><div class="col docItemCol_z5aJ"><div class="docItemContainer_c0TR"><article><nav class="theme-doc-breadcrumbs breadcrumbsContainer_Z_bl" aria-label="Breadcrumbs"><ul class="breadcrumbs"><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/weaviate/manage-objects"><span>How-to: Manage objects</span></a></li><li class="breadcrumbs__item breadcrumbs__item--active"><span class="breadcrumbs__link">Batch import</span></li></ul></nav><div class="tocCollapsible_ETCw theme-doc-toc-mobile tocMobile_ITEo"><button type="button" class="clean-btn tocCollapsibleButton_TO0P">On this page</button></div><div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><header><h1>Batch import</h1></header><p><a class="" href="/weaviate/tutorials/import">Batch imports</a> are an efficient way to add multiple data objects and cross-references.</p>
<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary>Additional information</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><p>To create a bulk import job, follow these steps:</p><ol>
<li class="">Initialize a batch object.</li>
<li class="">Add items to the batch object.</li>
<li class="">Ensure that the last batch is sent (flushed).</li>
</ol></div></div></details>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="basic-import">Basic import<a href="#basic-import" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Basic import" title="Direct link to Basic import" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>The following example adds objects to the <code>MyCollection</code> collection.</p>

style="color:#393A34">)</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div><div class="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-2"></div></div><h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="error-handling">Error handling<a href="#error-handling" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Error handling" title="Direct link to Error handling" translate="no">​</a></h3><p>During a batch import, any failed objects or references will be stored and can be obtained through <code>batch.failed_objects</code> and <code>batch.failed_references</code>.
Additionally, a running count of failed objects and references is maintained and can be accessed through <code>batch.number_errors</code> within the context manager.
This counter can be used to stop the import process in order to investigate the failed objects or references.</p><p>Find out more about error handling on the Python client <a class="" href="/weaviate/client-libraries/python">reference page</a>.</p></div></div><div class="tabPanel_nEcw tabPanelHidden_Ugst" style="display:none" aria-hidden="true"><div role="tabpanel" <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="server-side-batching">Server-side batching<a href="#server-side-batching" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Server-side batching" title="Direct link to Server-side batching" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-caution admonition_xJq3 alert alert--warning"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8.893 1.5c-.183-.31-.52-.5-.887-.5s-.703.19-.886.5L.138 13.499a.98.98 0 0 0 0 1.001c.193.31.53.501.886.501h13.964c.367 0 .704-.19.877-.5a1.03 1.03 0 0 0 .01-1.002L8.893 1.5zm.133 11.497H6.987v-2.003h2.039v2.003zm0-3.004H6.987V5.987h2.039v4.006z"></path></svg></span>Preview</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Server-side batching was added in <strong><code>v1.34</code></strong> as a <strong>preview</strong>.<br><br>
This means that the feature is still under development and may change in future releases, including potential breaking changes.
<strong>We do not recommend using this feature in production environments at this time.</strong></p></div></div>
<p>Here&#x27;s how to import objects into a collection named <code>MyCollection</code> using <a class="" href="/weaviate/concepts/data-import#server-side-batching">server-side batch imports</a>. The client will send data in batch sizes using feedback from the server.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="use-the-grpc-api">Use the gRPC API<a href="#use-the-grpc-api" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Use the gRPC API" title="Direct link to Use the gRPC API" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Added in <code>v1.23</code>.</div></div>
<p>The <a class="" href="/weaviate/api">gRPC API</a> is faster than the REST API. Use the gRPC API to improve import speeds.</p>
<div class="codeDropdownContainer_uCK5 code"><div class="codeDropdownHeader_PNgx"><div class="leftSection_ieqF"><span class="languageLabel_LeYV"></span><div class="languageSelector_Mp0Y"><select class="languageDropdown_BTMK"><option value="py" selected="">Python</option><option value="ts">JavaScript/TypeScript</option><option value="java6">Java v6</option><option value="java">Java v5 (Deprecated)</option><option value="go">Go</option><option value="csharp">C# (Beta)</option><option value="spark">Spark</option></select><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="" class="languageIcon_e8S9"><svg class="dropdownArrow_T7wX" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M5.293 7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0L10 10.586l3.293-3.293a1 1 0 111.414 1.414l-4 4a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 010-1.414z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div><div class="rightSection__3jI"><a href="https://weaviate-python-client.readthedocs.io/en/stable" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="apiDocsLink_EDfG" title="View API documentation"><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="py docs" height="12" width="12" style="vertical-align:middle"><span style="vertical-align:middle">  API docs</span></a><div class="versionInfo_e5Um"><span class="versionLabel_YSKW">More info<span class="tooltip_vwsi"><svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" class="infoIcon_bJII"><path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"></path></svg><span class="tooltipContent_QizM" data-position="left">Code snippets in the documentation reflect the latest client library and Weaviate Database version. Check the<!-- --> <a href="/weaviate/release-notes">Release notes</a> <!-- -->for specific versions.<br><br>If a snippet doesn&#x27;t work or you have feedback, please open a<!-- --> <a href="https://github.com/weaviate/docs/issues/new?template=doc_feedback.yml&amp;title=%5BDocumentation+Feedback%5D%3A+&amp;labels=user-feedback&amp;page-url=" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">GitHub issue</a>.</span></span></span></div></div></div><div class="codeContent_E0WP"><div class="tabPanel_nEcw" style="display:block" aria-hidden="false"><div role="tabpanel" class="tabItem_Ymn6"><p>The Python client uses gRPC by default.</p><br><p>The legacy Python client does not support gRPC.</p></div></div><div class="tabPanel_nEcw tabPanelHidden_Ugst" style="display:none" aria-hidden="true"><div role="tabpanel" class="tabItem_Ymn6"><p>The TypeScript client v3 uses gRPC by default.</p><br><p>The legacy TypeScript client does not support gRPC.</p></div></div><div class="tabPanel_nEcw tabPanelHidden_Ugst" style="display:none" aria-hidden="true"><div role="tabpanel" class="tabItem_Ymn6"><p>The Java client v6 uses gRPC by default.</p></div></div><div class="tabPanel_nEcw tabPanelHidden_Ugst" style="display:none" aria-hidden="true"><div role="tabpanel" class="tabItem_Ymn6"><p>To use the gRPC API with the Java client, add the <code>setGRPCHost</code> field to your client connection code. <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="specify-an-id-value">Specify an ID value<a href="#specify-an-id-value" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Specify an ID value" title="Direct link to Specify an ID value" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Weaviate generates an UUID for each object. Object IDs must be unique. If you set object IDs, use one of these deterministic UUID methods to prevent duplicate IDs:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>generate_uuid5</code> (Python)</li>
<li class=""><code>generateUuid5</code> (TypeScript)</li>
</ul>
<div class="codeDropdownContainer_uCK5 code"><div class="codeDropdownHeader_PNgx"><div class="leftSection_ieqF"><span class="languageLabel_LeYV"></span><div class="languageSelector_Mp0Y"><select class="languageDropdown_BTMK"><option value="py" selected="">Python</option><option value="ts">JavaScript/TypeScript</option><option value="go">Go</option><option value="java6">Java v6</option><option value="java">Java v5 (Deprecated)</option><option value="csharp">C# (Beta)</option></select><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="" class="languageIcon_e8S9"><svg class="dropdownArrow_T7wX" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M5.293 7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0L10 10.586l3.293-3.293a1 1 0 111.414 1.414l-4 4a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 010-1.414z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div><div class="rightSection__3jI"><a href="https://weaviate-python-client.readthedocs.io/en/stable" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="apiDocsLink_EDfG" title="View API documentation"><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="py docs" height="12" width="12" style="vertical-align:middle"><span style="vertical-align:middle">  API docs</span></a><div class="versionInfo_e5Um"><span class="versionLabel_YSKW">More info<span class="tooltip_vwsi"><svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" class="infoIcon_bJII"><path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"></path></svg><span class="tooltipContent_QizM" data-position="left">Code snippets in the documentation reflect the latest client library and Weaviate Database version. Check the<!-- --> <a href="/weaviate/release-notes">Release notes</a> <!-- -->for specific versions.<br><br>If a snippet doesn&#x27;t work or you have feedback, please open a<!-- --> <a href="https://github.com/weaviate/docs/issues/new?template=doc_feedback.yml&amp;title=%5BDocumentation+Feedback%5D%3A+&amp;labels=user-feedback&amp;page-url=" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">GitHub issue</a>.</span></span></span></div></div></div><div class="codeContent_E0WP"><div class="tabPanel_nEcw" style="display:block" aria-hidden="false"><div role="tabpanel" class="tabItem_Ymn6"><div><div class="language-py codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_QJqH"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-py codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line theme-code-block-highlighted-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">from</span><span class="token plain"> weaviate</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token plain">util </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">import</span><span class="token plain"> generate_uuid5  </span><span class="token <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="specify-a-vector">Specify a vector<a href="#specify-a-vector" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Specify a vector" title="Direct link to Specify a vector" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Use the <code>vector</code> property to specify a vector for each object.</p>

style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div><div class="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-2"></div></div></div></div></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="specify-named-vectors">Specify named vectors<a href="#specify-named-vectors" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Specify named vectors" title="Direct link to Specify named vectors" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Added in <code>v1.24</code></div></div>
<p>When you create an object, you can specify named vectors (if <a class="" href="/weaviate/manage-collections/vector-config#define-named-vectors">configured in your collection</a>).</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="import-with-references">Import with references<a href="#import-with-references" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Import with references" title="Direct link to Import with references" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>You can batch create links from an object to another other object through cross-references.</p>
<div class="codeDropdownContainer_uCK5 code"><div class="codeDropdownHeader_PNgx"><div class="leftSection_ieqF"><span class="languageLabel_LeYV"></span><div class="languageSelector_Mp0Y"><select class="languageDropdown_BTMK"><option value="py" selected="">Python</option><option value="java6">Java v6</option><option value="csharp">C# (Beta)</option></select><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="" class="languageIcon_e8S9"><svg class="dropdownArrow_T7wX" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M5.293 7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0L10 10.586l3.293-3.293a1 1 0 111.414 1.414l-4 4a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 010-1.414z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div><div class="rightSection__3jI"><a href="https://weaviate-python-client.readthedocs.io/en/stable" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="apiDocsLink_EDfG" title="View API documentation"><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="py docs" height="12" width="12" style="vertical-align:middle"><span style="vertical-align:middle">  API docs</span></a><div class="versionInfo_e5Um"><span class="versionLabel_YSKW">More info<span class="tooltip_vwsi"><svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" class="infoIcon_bJII"><path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"></path></svg><span class="tooltipContent_QizM" data-position="left">Code snippets in the documentation reflect the latest client library and Weaviate Database version. <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="python-specific-considerations">Python-specific considerations<a href="#python-specific-considerations" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Python-specific considerations" title="Direct link to Python-specific considerations" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>The Python clients have built-in batching methods to help you optimize import speed. For details, see the client documentation:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><a class="" href="/weaviate/client-libraries/python/notes-best-practices">Python client</a></li>
</ul>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="async-python-client-and-batching">Async Python client and batching<a href="#async-python-client-and-batching" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Async Python client and batching" title="Direct link to Async Python client and batching" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>Currently, the <a class="" href="/weaviate/client-libraries/python/async#bulk-data-insertion">async Python client does not support batching</a>. To use batching, use the sync Python client.</p>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="stream-data-from-large-files">Stream data from large files<a href="#stream-data-from-large-files" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Stream data from large files" title="Direct link to Stream data from large files" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>If your dataset is large, consider streaming the import to avoid out-of-memory issues.</p>
<p>To try the example code, download the sample data and create the sample input files.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="batch-vectorization">Batch vectorization<a href="#batch-vectorization" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Batch vectorization" title="Direct link to Batch vectorization" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Added in <code>v1.25</code>.</div></div>
<!-- -->
<p>Some <a class="" href="/weaviate/model-providers">model providers</a> provide batch vectorization APIs, where each request can include multiple objects.</p>
<p>From Weaviate <code>v1.25.0</code>, a batch import automatically makes use of the model providers&#x27; batch vectorization APIs where available. This reduces the number of requests to the model provider, improving throughput.</p>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="model-provider-configurations">Model provider configurations<a href="#model-provider-configurations" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Model provider configurations" title="Direct link to Model provider configurations" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>You can configure the batch vectorization settings for each model provider, such as the requests per minute or tokens per minute. The following examples sets rate limits for Cohere and OpenAI integrations, and provides API keys for both.</p>
<p>Note that each provider exposes different configuration options.</p>

class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        requests_per_minute_embeddings</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token plain">rpm_embeddings</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain">   </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># e.g. OpenAI also exposes tokens per minute for embeddings</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span aria-hidden="true"><div role="tabpanel" class="tabItem_Ymn6"><div><div class="language-java codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="additional-considerations">Additional considerations<a href="#additional-considerations" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Additional considerations" title="Direct link to Additional considerations" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Data imports can be resource intensive. Consider the following when you import large amounts of data.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="asynchronous-imports">Asynchronous imports<a href="#asynchronous-imports" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Asynchronous imports" title="Direct link to Asynchronous imports" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-caution admonition_xJq3 alert alert--warning"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8.893 1.5c-.183-.31-.52-.5-.887-.5s-.703.19-.886.5L.138 13.499a.98.98 0 0 0 0 1.001c.193.31.53.501.886.501h13.964c.367 0 .704-.19.877-.5a1.03 1.03 0 0 0 .01-1.002L8.893 1.5zm.133 11.497H6.987v-2.003h2.039v2.003zm0-3.004H6.987V5.987h2.039v4.006z"></path></svg></span>Experimental</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Available starting in <code>v1.22</code>. This is an experimental feature. Use with caution.</p></div></div>
<p>To maximize import speed, enable <a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/indexing/vector-index#asynchronous-indexing">asynchronous indexing</a>.</p>
<p>To enable asynchronous indexing, set the <code>ASYNC_INDEXING</code> environment variable to <code>true</code> in your Weaviate configuration file.</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_QJqH"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">weaviate</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">image</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> cr.weaviate.io/semitechnologies/weaviate</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">1.34.4</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">...</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">environment</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">ASYNC_INDEXING</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;true&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">...</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="automatically-add-new-tenants">Automatically add new tenants<a href="#automatically-add-new-tenants" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Automatically add new tenants" title="Direct link to Automatically add new tenants" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<!-- -->
<p>By default, Weaviate returns an error if you try to insert an object into a non-existent tenant. To change this behavior so Weaviate creates a new tenant, set <code>autoTenantCreation</code> to <code>true</code> in the collection definition.</p>
<p>The auto-tenant feature is available from <code>v1.25.0</code> for batch imports, and from <code>v1.25.2</code> for single object insertions as well.</p>
<p>Set <code>autoTenantCreation</code> when you create the collection, or reconfigure the collection to update the setting as needed.</p>
<p>Automatic tenant creation is useful when you import a large number of objects. Be cautious if your data is likely to have small inconsistencies or typos. For example, the names <code>TenantOne</code>, <code>tenantOne</code>, and <code>TenntOne</code> will create three different tenants.</p>
<p>For details, see <a class="" href="/weaviate/manage-collections/multi-tenancy#automatically-add-new-tenants">auto-tenant</a>.</p>
